    <script>
        // Set current date
        document.querySelector('.current-date').textContent = new Date().toLocaleDateString('id-ID', {
            weekday: 'long',
            year: 'numeric',
            month: 'long',
            day: 'numeric'
        });
        
        // Fungsi logout sederhana
        function logoutUser() {
            if (confirm('Apakah Anda yakin ingin logout?')) {
                // Hapus data sesi
                localStorage.removeItem('user');
                localStorage.removeItem('loginTime');
                
                // Redirect ke halaman login
                window.location.href = 'index.html';
            }
        }
        
        // Atur event listener untuk tombol logout
        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
            const logoutBtn = document.querySelector('.logout-btn');
            if (logoutBtn) {
                logoutBtn.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                    e.preventDefault();
                    logoutUser();
                });
            }
            
            // File upload functionality
            const lpjFile = document.getElementById('lpjFile');
            const browseFileBtn = document.getElementById('browseFileBtn');
            const fileUploadSection = document.getElementById('fileUploadSection');
            const fileName = document.getElementById('fileName');
            const fileSize = document.getElementById('fileSize');
            
            browseFileBtn.addEventListener('click', function() {
                lpjFile.click();
            });
            
            fileUploadSection.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                if (e.target !== browseFileBtn && !browseFileBtn.contains(e.target)) {
                    lpjFile.click();
                }
            });
            
            fileUploadSection.addEventListener('dragover', function(e) {
                e.preventDefault();
                fileUploadSection.style.borderColor = '#667eea';
                fileUploadSection.style.backgroundColor = '#f0f5ff';
            });
            
            fileUploadSection.addEventListener('dragleave', function(e) {
                e.preventDefault();
                fileUploadSection.style.borderColor = '#bdbdbd';
                fileUploadSection.style.backgroundColor = '#fafafa';
            });
            
            fileUploadSection.addEventListener('drop', function(e) {
                e.preventDefault();
                fileUploadSection.style.borderColor = '#bdbdbd';
                fileUploadSection.style.backgroundColor = '#fafafa';
                
                if (e.dataTransfer.files.length) {
                    lpjFile.files = e.dataTransfer.files;
                    updateFileInfo();
                }
            });
            
            lpjFile.addEventListener('change', updateFileInfo);
            
            function updateFileInfo() {
                if (lpjFile.files.length > 0) {
                    const file = lpjFile.files[0];
                    fileName.textContent = `File: ${file.name}`;
                    fileName.style.color = '#28a745';
                    
                    // Calculate file size
                    const sizeInMB = (file.size / (1024 * 1024)).toFixed(2);
                    fileSize.textContent = `Ukuran: ${sizeInMB} MB`;
                    
                    // Check if file is PDF
                    if (file.type !== 'application/pdf') {
                        alert('Hanya file PDF yang diperbolehkan!');
                        lpjFile.value = '';
                        fileName.textContent = '';
                        fileSize.textContent = '';
                    }
                    
                    // Check file size (max 1GB = 1024 MB)
                    if (file.size > 1024 * 1024 * 1024) {
                        alert('File terlalu besar! Maksimal 1GB.');
                        lpjFile.value = '';
                        fileName.textContent = '';
                        fileSize.textContent = '';
                    }
                } else {
                    fileName.textContent = '';
                    fileSize.textContent = '';
                }
            }
            
            // View and Download functionality
            document.querySelectorAll('.table-container .btn-secondary').forEach(button => {
                button.addEventListener('click', function() {
                    const row = this.closest('tr');
                    const tahun = row.cells[0].textContent;
                    const kegiatan = row.cells[1].textContent;
                    const file = row.cells[3].textContent;
                    
                    if (this.querySelector('.fa-eye')) {
                        alert(`Melihat LPJ:\n\nTahun: ${tahun}\nKegiatan: ${kegiatan}\nFile: ${file}`);
                    } else if (this.querySelector('.fa-download')) {
                        alert(`Mengunduh LPJ:\n\nTahun: ${tahun}\nKegiatan: ${kegiatan}\nFile: ${file}\n\n(Simulasi download)`);
                    }
                });
            });
            
            // Form submission
            document.getElementById('uploadLpjForm').addEventListener('submit', function(e) {
                e.preventDefault();
                
                const tahun = document.getElementById('tahunLpj').value;
                const kegiatan = document.getElementById('jenisKegiatan').value;
                const kegiatanText = document.getElementById('jenisKegiatan').options[document.getElementById('jenisKegiatan').selectedIndex].text;
                
                if (!lpjFile.files.length) {
                    alert('Harap pilih file LPJ & K!');
                    return;
                }
                
                if (!tahun || !kegiatan) {
                    alert('Harap lengkapi tahun dan jenis kegiatan!');
                    return;
                }
                
                // Simulate file upload
                const file = lpjFile.files[0];
                const sizeInMB = (file.size / (1024 * 1024)).toFixed(2);
                
                if (confirm(`Apakah Anda yakin mengarsipkan LPJ & K untuk tahun ${tahun} - ${kegiatanText}?\n\nFile: ${file.name}\nUkuran: ${sizeInMB} MB`)) {
                    alert('LPJ & K berhasil diarsipkan! File telah tersimpan dalam sistem.');
                    
                    // Reset form
                    this.reset();
                    fileName.textContent = '';
                    fileSize.textContent = '';
                    
                    // Set default year to 2025
                    document.getElementById('tahunLpj').value = '2025';
                }
            });
        });
    </script>
</body>
</html>
```

---

    <script>
        // Set current date
        document.querySelector('.current-date').textContent = new Date().toLocaleDateString('id-ID', {
            weekday: 'long',
            year: 'numeric',
            month: 'long',
            day: 'numeric'
        });
        
        // Fungsi logout sederhana
        function logoutUser() {
            if (confirm('Apakah Anda yakin ingin logout?')) {
                // Hapus data sesi
                localStorage.removeItem('user');
                localStorage.removeItem('loginTime');
                
                // Redirect ke halaman login
                window.location.href = 'index.html';
            }
        }
        
        // Atur event listener untuk tombol logout
        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
            const logoutBtn = document.querySelector('.logout-btn');
            if (logoutBtn) {
                logoutBtn.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                    e.preventDefault();
                    logoutUser();
                });
            }
            
            const userData = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('user'));
            if (userData && userData.roleType === 'pembina') {
                document.querySelectorAll('.ukm-name').forEach(el => {
                    el.textContent = userData.ukm;
                });
            }
        });
    </script>
</body>
</html>
```

---

### 5.2. laporan-ormawa.html
```html
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="id">
<head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8">
    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0">
    <title>Laporan UKM - Sistem Transparansi Dana UKM</title>
    <style>
        /* Base Styles from Original Admin Dashboard */
        * {
            margin: 0;

            font-family: 'Poppins', sans-serif;
        }
        
        body {
            background: #f5f7fa;
            color: #333;
            overflow-x: hidden;
        }
        
        .dashboard-container {
            display: flex;
            min-height: 100vh;
            width: 100%;
        }
        
        /* Sidebar Styles */
        .sidebar {
            width: 260px;
            background: linear-gradient(180deg, #1a237e 0%, #283593 100%);
            color: white;

            position: fixed;
            height: 100vh;
            overflow-y: auto;
            z-index: 1000;
            box-shadow: 2px 0 10px rgba(0,0,0,0.1);
        }
        
        .sidebar-header {
            padding: 0 20px 20px;
            border-bottom: 1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.1);
            margin-bottom: 20px;
        }
        
        .sidebar-header h2 {
            font-size: 18px;
            font-weight: 600;
            margin-bottom: 8px;
            color: white;
        }
        
        .role-badge {
            display: inline-block;
            background: rgba(255,255,255,0.2);
            padding: 4px 12px;
            border-radius: 20px;
            font-size: 12px;
            margin-bottom: 10px;
        }
        
        .current-date {
            font-size: 12px;
            opacity: 0.8;
            color: rgba(255,255,255,0.7) !important;
            margin-top: 10px;
        }
        
        .sidebar-nav ul {
            list-style: none;

    <script>
        // Set current date
        document.querySelector('.current-date').textContent = new Date().toLocaleDateString('id-ID', {
            weekday: 'long',
            year: 'numeric',
            month: 'long',
            day: 'numeric'
        });
        
        // Fungsi logout sederhana
        function logoutUser() {
            if (confirm('Apakah Anda yakin ingin logout?')) {
                // Hapus data sesi
                localStorage.removeItem('user');
                localStorage.removeItem('loginTime');
                
                // Redirect ke halaman login
                window.location.href = 'index.html';
            }
        }
        
        // Atur event listener
        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
            // Logout
            const logoutBtn = document.querySelector('.logout-btn');
            if (logoutBtn) {
                logoutBtn.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                    e.preventDefault();
                    logoutUser();
                });
            }
            
            // User data
            const userData = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('user'));
            if (userData && userData.roleType === 'pembina') {
                document.querySelectorAll('.ukm-name').forEach(el => {
                    el.textContent = userData.ukm;
                });
            }
            
            // Generate Report
            document.getElementById('generateReport').addEventListener('click', function() {
                const tahun = document.getElementById('periode').value;
                const kegiatan = document.getElementById('kegiatanFilter').value;
                
                alert(`Membuat laporan untuk tahun ${tahun} ${kegiatan !== 'all' ? `- kegiatan: ${kegiatan}` : ''}...`);
            });
            
            // Export Report
            document.getElementById('exportReport').addEventListener('click', function() {
                const format = document.getElementById('exportType').value;
                const range = document.getElementById('exportRange').value;
                
                alert(`Laporan berhasil diexport dalam format ${format} (${range})!`);
            });
            
            // View transaction details
            document.querySelectorAll('.btn-action-pembina').forEach(btn => {
                btn.addEventListener('click', function() {
                    if (this.innerHTML.includes('fa-eye')) {
                        const row = this.closest('tr');
                        const transaksiId = row.cells[0].textContent;
                        const kegiatan = row.cells[2].textContent;
                        const jumlah = row.cells[4].textContent;
                        alert(`Detail Transaksi:\nID: ${transaksiId}\nKegiatan: ${kegiatan}\nJumlah: ${jumlah}`);
                    } else if (this.innerHTML.includes('fa-search')) {
                        alert('Membuka halaman review LPJ...');
                    } else if (this.innerHTML.includes('fa-download')) {
                        alert('Mendownload file LPJ...');
                    }
                });
            });
        });
    </script>
</body>
</html>
```

---

    <script>
        // Set current date
        document.querySelector('.current-date').textContent = new Date().toLocaleDateString('id-ID', {
            weekday: 'long',
            year: 'numeric',
            month: 'long',
            day: 'numeric'
        });
        
        // Fungsi logout sederhana
        function logoutUser() {
            if (confirm('Apakah Anda yakin ingin logout?')) {
                // Hapus data sesi
                localStorage.removeItem('user');
                localStorage.removeItem('loginTime');
                
                // Redirect ke halaman login
                window.location.href = 'index.html';
            }
        }
        
        // Atur event listener
        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
            // Logout
            const logoutBtn = document.querySelector('.logout-btn');
            if (logoutBtn) {
                logoutBtn.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                    e.preventDefault();
                    logoutUser();
                });
            }
            
            // User data
            const userData = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('user'));
            if (userData && userData.roleType === 'pembina') {
                document.querySelectorAll('.ukm-name').forEach(el => {
                    el.textContent = userData.ukm;
                });
            }
            
            // Apply Filter
            document.getElementById('applyFilter').addEventListener('click', function() {
                const status = document.getElementById('filterStatus').value;
                const periode = document.getElementById('filterPeriode').value;
                alert(`Filter diterapkan: Status ${status}, Tahun ${periode}`);
            });
            
            // Export LPJ List
            document.getElementById('exportLpjList').addEventListener('click', function() {
                alert('Daftar LPJ berhasil diexport ke Excel!');
            });
            
            // Review buttons
            const startReviewBtns = document.querySelectorAll('.start-review, .view-details');
            const reviewForm = document.getElementById('reviewForm');
            const reviewTitle = document.getElementById('reviewTitle');
            const cancelReviewBtn = document.getElementById('cancelReview');
            
            startReviewBtns.forEach(btn => {
                btn.addEventListener('click', function() {
                    const lpjId = this.getAttribute('data-id');
                    const tahun = this.closest('tr').querySelector('td:nth-child(2)').textContent;
                    reviewForm.style.display = 'block';
                    reviewTitle.textContent = `Review LPJ & K - Tahun ${tahun}`;
                    document.getElementById('lpjFileName').textContent = `LPJ_U2M_${tahun}.pdf`;
                    reviewForm.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth' });
                });
            });
            
            // Cancel Review
            cancelReviewBtn.addEventListener('click', function() {
                if (confirm('Batalkan review? Semua perubahan yang belum disimpan akan hilang.')) {
                    reviewForm.style.display = 'none';
                    document.getElementById('reviewComments').value = '';
                    document.getElementById('reviewStatus').value = '';
                    document.querySelectorAll('.criteria-checkbox-pembina').forEach(cb => cb.checked = false);
                    document.querySelectorAll('.criteria-item-pembina').forEach(item => item.classList.remove('checked'));
                }
            });
            
            // Download LPJ
            document.getElementById('downloadLpj').addEventListener('click', function() {
                alert('File LPJ sedang didownload...');
            });
            
            // View LPJ Online
            document.getElementById('viewLpjOnline').addEventListener('click', function() {
                alert('Membuka LPJ di tab baru...');
            });
            
            // Save Draft
            document.getElementById('saveDraft').addEventListener('click', function() {
                alert('Review disimpan sebagai draft!');
            });
            
            // Submit Review
            document.getElementById('submitReview').addEventListener('click', function() {
                const comments = document.getElementById('reviewComments').value;
                const status = document.getElementById('reviewStatus').value;
                
                if (!comments || !status) {
                    alert('Harap lengkapi komentar dan pilih status review!');
                    return;
                }
                
                const checkedCriteria = document.querySelectorAll('.criteria-checkbox-pembina:checked').length;
                if (checkedCriteria < 3) {
                    alert('Harap centang minimal 3 kriteria sebelum submit review!');
                    return;
                }
                
                if (confirm(`Apakah Anda yakin submit review dengan status "${status}"?`)) {
                    alert('Review berhasil disubmit! LPJ akan diproses ke Admin Keuangan.');
                    reviewForm.style.display = 'none';
                    document.getElementById('reviewComments').value = '';
                    document.getElementById('reviewStatus').value = '';
                    document.querySelectorAll('.criteria-checkbox-pembina').forEach(cb => cb.checked = false);
                    document.querySelectorAll('.criteria-item-pembina').forEach(item => item.classList.remove('checked'));
                }
            });
            
            // Criteria checkboxes
            document.querySelectorAll('.criteria-checkbox-pembina').forEach(checkbox => {
                checkbox.addEventListener('change', function() {
                    const criteriaItem = this.closest('.criteria-item-pembina');
                    if (this.checked) {
                        criteriaItem.classList.add('checked');
                    } else {
                        criteriaItem.classList.remove('checked');
                    }
                });
            });
        });
    </script>
</body>
</html>
```

---

    <script>
        // Set current date
        document.querySelector('.current-date').textContent = new Date().toLocaleDateString('id-ID', {
            weekday: 'long',
            year: 'numeric',
            month: 'long',
            day: 'numeric'
        });
        
        // Fungsi logout sederhana
        function logoutUser() {
            if (confirm('Apakah Anda yakin ingin logout?')) {
                // Hapus data sesi
                localStorage.removeItem('user');
                localStorage.removeItem('loginTime');
                
                // Redirect ke halaman login
                window.location.href = 'index.html';
            }
        }
        
        // Atur event listener
        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
            // Logout
            const logoutBtn = document.querySelector('.logout-btn');
            if (logoutBtn) {
                logoutBtn.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                    e.preventDefault();
                    logoutUser();
                });
            }
            
            // User data
            const userData = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('user'));
            if (userData && userData.roleType === 'pembina') {
                document.querySelectorAll('.ukm-name').forEach(el => {
                    el.textContent = userData.ukm;
                });
            }
            
            // Search Transactions
            document.getElementById('searchTransactions').addEventListener('click', function() {
                const year = document.getElementById('filterYear').value;
                const month = document.getElementById('filterMonth').value;
                const type = document.getElementById('filterType').value;
                
                let monthText = month === 'all' ? 'Semua Bulan' : 
                    month === '01' ? 'Januari' :
                    month === '02' ? 'Februari' :
                    month === '10' ? 'Oktober' :
                    month === '11' ? 'November' : 'Desember';
                
                let typeText = type === 'all' ? 'Semua Jenis' :
                    type === 'income' ? 'Pemasukan' : 'Pengeluaran';
                
                alert(`Mencari transaksi:\nTahun: ${year}\nBulan: ${monthText}\nJenis: ${typeText}`);
                
                // Update table title
                const tableTitle = document.querySelector('.table-title-pembina');
                if (month !== 'all') {
                    tableTitle.textContent = `Detail Transaksi ${monthText} ${year}`;
                } else {
                    tableTitle.textContent = `Detail Transaksi Tahun ${year}`;
                }
            });
            
            // View transaction details
            document.querySelectorAll('.btn-view-detail').forEach(btn => {
                btn.addEventListener('click', function() {
                    const transactionId = this.getAttribute('data-id');
                    const row = this.closest('tr');
                    const date = row.cells[0].textContent;
                    const description = row.cells[2].textContent;
                    const type = row.cells[3].textContent;
                    const amount = row.cells[4].textContent;
                    const status = row.cells[5].querySelector('.status').textContent;
                    
                    // Create modal-like alert
                    const detail = `
Detail Transaksi:
-------------------------
ID Transaksi: ${transactionId}
Tanggal: ${date}
Keterangan: ${description}
Jenis: ${type}
Jumlah: ${amount}
Status: ${status}
-------------------------
Lampiran: Bukti_transaksi_${transactionId}.pdf
Kegiatan: ${description.includes('-') ? description.split('-')[1].trim() : 'General'}
Diupload: ${date} oleh Bendahara UKM
`;
                    
                    alert(detail);
                });
            });
            
            // Pagination buttons
            document.querySelectorAll('.btn-action-pembina').forEach(btn => {
                if (btn.innerHTML.includes('fa-chevron')) {
                    btn.addEventListener('click', function() {
                        if (this.innerHTML.includes('fa-chevron-left')) {
                            alert('Navigasi ke halaman sebelumnya...');
                        } else {
                            alert('Navigasi ke halaman berikutnya...');
                        }
                    });
                }
            });
        });
    </script>
</body>
</html>
```

---

### 5.5. log-audit.html
```html

        /* Main Content Styles */

        document.querySelector('.current-date').textContent = new Date().toLocaleDateString('id-ID', {
            weekday: 'long',
            year: 'numeric',
            month: 'long',
            day: 'numeric'
        });
        
        // Fungsi logout sederhana
        function logoutUser() {
            if (confirm('Apakah Anda yakin ingin logout?')) {
                // Hapus data sesi
                localStorage.removeItem('user');
                localStorage.removeItem('loginTime');
                
                // Redirect ke halaman login
                window.location.href = 'index.html';
            }
        }
        
        // Data audit detail
        const auditData = {
            "AUD2025003": {
                title: "Audit Semester II 2025 - UKM U2M",
                date: "28 Oktober 2025",
                period: "Semester II 2025 (Juli - Desember 2025)",
                auditor: "Admin Keuangan 1 - Dr. Surya Adi, M.Ak.",
                status: "warning",
                complianceRate: "85%",
                summary: "Audit menemukan 3 temuan minor yang perlu diperbaiki dalam pengelolaan keuangan UKM U2M. Secara keseluruhan, pengelolaan keuangan sudah cukup baik namun perlu perhatian pada dokumentasi transaksi.",
                findings: [
                    {
                        id: 1,
                        title: "Dokumentasi Bukti Transaksi Tidak Lengkap",

                        category: "minor",

                    },
                    {

                    }

                ]
            },
            "AUD2025002": {
                title: "Audit Semester I 2025 - UKM U2M",
                date: "15 Juli 2025",

                status: "compliant",
                complianceRate: "98%",
                summary: "Tidak ditemukan penyimpangan yang signifikan dalam pengelolaan keuangan UKM U2M. Semua transaksi terdokumentasi dengan baik dan sesuai dengan prosedur yang berlaku.",
                findings: [
                    {
                        id: 1,
                        title: "Tidak Ada Temuan Signifikan",
                        description: "Pengelolaan keuangan UKM U2M untuk periode Semester I 2025 berjalan dengan baik sesuai standar dan prosedur yang berlaku.",
                        category: "compliant",

            "AUD2024004": {
                title: "Audit Akhir Tahun 2024 - UKM U2M",

                period: "Tahun 2024 (Januari - Desember 2024)",

                status: "non-compliant",
                complianceRate: "65%",
                summary: "Ditemukan 1 temuan mayor terkait ketidaksesuaian antara laporan keuangan dengan bukti transaksi. Perlu perbaikan segera sebelum audit berikutnya.",
                findings: [
                    {
                        id: 1,
                        title: "Ketidaksesuaian Laporan Keuangan",

                period: "Semester I 2024 (Januari - Juni 2024)",

                status: "compliant",
                complianceRate: "95%",
                summary: "Pengelolaan keuangan berjalan dengan baik. Hanya ditemukan sedikit ketidaksesuaian dokumentasi yang sudah diperbaiki selama audit.",
                findings: [
                    {
                        id: 1,
                        title: "Dokumentasi Lengkap dan Teratur",
                        description: "Semua transaksi terdokumentasi dengan baik dan sesuai prosedur.",
                        category: "compliant",
                        recommendation: "Pertahankan kualitas dokumentasi yang sudah baik."
                    }
                ],
                recommendations: [
                    "Pertahankan sistem yang sudah berjalan baik",
                    "Tingkatkan frekuensi pemeriksaan internal"
                ]

        // Atur event listener
        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
            // Logout
            const logoutBtn = document.querySelector('.logout-btn');
            if (logoutBtn) {
                logoutBtn.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                    e.preventDefault();
                    logoutUser();
                });
            }
            
            // User data
            const userData = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('user'));
            if (userData && userData.roleType === 'pembina') {
                document.querySelectorAll('.ukm-name').forEach(el => {
                    el.textContent = userData.ukm;
                });
            }
            
            // Apply Filter
            document.getElementById('applyFilter').addEventListener('click', function() {
                const year = document.getElementById('filterYear').value;
                const status = document.getElementById('filterStatus').value;
                const auditor = document.getElementById('filterAuditor').value;
                
                let statusText = status === 'all' ? 'Semua Status' : 
                    status === 'compliant' ? 'Bersih' :
                    status === 'warning' ? 'Perhatian' : 'Temuan';
                
                let auditorText = auditor === 'all' ? 'Semua Auditor' :
                    auditor === 'admin1' ? 'Admin Keuangan 1' : 'Admin Keuangan 2';
                
                alert(`Filter diterapkan:\nTahun: ${year}\nStatus: ${statusText}\nAuditor: ${auditorText}`);
            });
            
            // Export Audit
            document.getElementById('exportAudit').addEventListener('click', function() {
                alert('Laporan audit berhasil diexport ke format PDF!');
            });
            
            // Modal elements
            const modal = document.getElementById('auditModal');
            const modalTitle = document.getElementById('modalTitle');
            const modalBody = document.getElementById('modalBody');
            const closeModal = document.getElementById('closeModal');
            
            // View audit details
            document.querySelectorAll('.btn-view-audit').forEach(btn => {
                btn.addEventListener('click', function() {
                    const auditId = this.getAttribute('data-id');
                    const audit = auditData[auditId];
                    
                    if (audit) {
                        modalTitle.textContent = audit.title;
                        modalBody.innerHTML = generateAuditDetailHTML(audit);
                        modal.style.display = 'flex';
                    }
                });
            });
            
            // Close modal
            closeModal.addEventListener('click', function() {
                modal.style.display = 'none';
            });
            
            // Close modal when clicking outside
            modal.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                if (e.target === modal) {
                    modal.style.display = 'none';
                }
            });
        });
        
        // Function to generate audit detail HTML
        function generateAuditDetailHTML(audit) {
            let statusClass = '';
            let statusText = '';
            
            switch(audit.status) {
                case 'compliant':
                    statusClass = 'status-compliant';
                    statusText = 'Bersih (Compliant)';
                    break;
                case 'warning':
                    statusClass = 'status-warning';
                    statusText = 'Perhatian (Warning)';
                    break;
                case 'non-compliant':
                    statusClass = 'status-non-compliant';
                    statusText = 'Temuan (Non-Compliant)';
                    break;
            }
            
            let findingsHTML = '';
            audit.findings.forEach(finding => {
                let findingClass = '';
                switch(finding.category) {
                    case 'compliant':
                        findingClass = 'compliant';
                        break;
                    case 'minor':
                        findingClass = '';
                        break;
                    case 'major':
                        findingClass = 'non-compliant';
                        break;
                }
                
                findingsHTML += `
                    <div class="audit-finding-item ${findingClass}">
                        <div class="audit-finding-title">
                            ${finding.category === 'major' ? '<i class="fas fa-exclamation-circle" style="color: #f44336;"></i>' : 
                              finding.category === 'minor' ? '<i class="fas fa-exclamation-triangle" style="color: #ff9800;"></i>' :
                              '<i class="fas fa-check-circle" style="color: #4caf50;"></i>'}
                            ${finding.title}
                        </div>
                        <div class="audit-finding-desc">${finding.description}</div>
                        <div class="audit-finding-recommendation">
                            <strong>Rekomendasi:</strong> ${finding.recommendation}
                        </div>
                    </div>
                `;
            });
            
            let recommendationsHTML = '';
            audit.recommendations.forEach((rec, index) => {
                recommendationsHTML += `<li>${rec}</li>`;
            });
            
            return `
                <div class="audit-detail-section">
                    <h4 class="audit-detail-title">Informasi Umum Audit</h4>
                    <div class="audit-detail-grid">
                        <div class="audit-detail-item">
                            <span class="audit-detail-label">Tanggal Audit</span>
                            <span class="audit-detail-value">${audit.date}</span>
                        </div>
                        <div class="audit-detail-item">
                            <span class="audit-detail-label">Periode Audit</span>
                            <span class="audit-detail-value">${audit.period}</span>
                        </div>
                        <div class="audit-detail-item">
                            <span class="audit-detail-label">Auditor</span>
                            <span class="audit-detail-value">${audit.auditor}</span>
                        </div>
                        <div class="audit-detail-item">
                            <span class="audit-detail-label">Status</span>
                            <span class="audit-detail-value"><span class="status ${statusClass}">${statusText}</span></span>
                        </div>
                        <div class="audit-detail-item">
                            <span class="audit-detail-label">Tingkat Kepatuhan</span>
                            <span class="audit-detail-value">${audit.complianceRate}</span>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                </div>
                
                <div class="audit-detail-section">
                    <h4 class="audit-detail-title">Ringkasan Audit</h4>
                    <div class="audit-summary-card">
                        <div class="audit-summary-text">${audit.summary}</div>
                    </div>
                </div>
                
                <div class="audit-detail-section">
                    <h4 class="audit-detail-title">Temuan Audit</h4>
                    <div class="audit-findings-list">
                        ${findingsHTML}
                    </div>
                </div>
                
                <div class="audit-detail-section">
                    <h4 class="audit-detail-title">Rekomendasi Umum</h4>
                    <div class="audit-summary-card">
                        <ol style="padding-left: 20px; color: #333;">
                            ${recommendationsHTML}
                        </ol>
                    </div>
                </div>
                
                <div class="audit-detail-section" style="text-align: center; margin-top: 30px;">
                    <button class="btn-apply-pembina" onclick="downloadAuditReport()">
                        <i class="fas fa-download"></i> Download Laporan Lengkap
                    </button>
                </div>
            `;
        }
        
        // Function to download audit report
        function downloadAuditReport() {
            alert('Laporan audit lengkap sedang didownload...');
        }
    </script>
</body>
</html>
```

        // Set current date
        document.querySelector('.current-date').textContent = new Date().toLocaleDateString('id-ID', {
            weekday: 'long',
            year: 'numeric',
            month: 'long',
            day: 'numeric'

        // Fungsi logout sederhana
function logoutUser() {
    if (confirm('Apakah Anda yakin ingin logout?')) {
        // Hapus data sesi
        localStorage.removeItem('user');
        localStorage.removeItem('loginTime');
        
        // Redirect ke halaman login
        window.location.href = 'index.html';
    }
}

// Atur event listener untuk tombol logout
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
    const logoutBtn = document.querySelector('.logout-btn');
    if (logoutBtn) {
        logoutBtn.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            logoutUser();
        });
    }
});
    </script>
</body>
</html>
```

        // Set current date
        document.querySelector('.current-date').textContent = new Date().toLocaleDateString('id-ID', {
            weekday: 'long',
            year: 'numeric',
            month: 'long',
            day: 'numeric'

        function tambahUKM() {
            alert('Fitur tambah UKM baru akan dibuka');
            // Implementasi modal/form tambah UKM
        }
        
        function exportData() {
            alert('Data UKM akan diexport ke Excel');
        }
        
        function importData() {
            alert('Fitur import data UKM');
        }
        
        // Tambahkan class btn-info untuk tombol eye
        const style = document.createElement('style');
        style.textContent = `
            .btn-info {
                background: linear-gradient(135deg, #3498db 0%, #2980b9 100%);
                color: white;
            }
            .btn-danger {
                background: linear-gradient(135deg, #e74c3c 0%, #c0392b 100%);
                color: white;
            }
        `;
        document.head.appendChild(style);
        
        // Fungsi logout sederhana
        function logoutUser() {
            if (confirm('Apakah Anda yakin ingin logout?')) {
                // Hapus data sesi
                localStorage.removeItem('user');
                localStorage.removeItem('loginTime');
                
                // Redirect ke halaman login
                window.location.href = 'index.html';
            }
        }
        
        // Atur event listener untuk tombol logout
        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
            const logoutBtn = document.querySelector('.logout-btn');
            if (logoutBtn) {
                logoutBtn.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                    e.preventDefault();
                    logoutUser();
                });
            }
        });
    </script>
</body>
</html>
```

        // Fungsi logout sederhana
function logoutUser() {
    if (confirm('Apakah Anda yakin ingin logout?')) {
        // Hapus data sesi
        localStorage.removeItem('user');
        localStorage.removeItem('loginTime');
        
        // Redirect ke halaman login
        window.location.href = 'index.html';
    }
}

// Atur event listener untuk tombol logout
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
    const logoutBtn = document.querySelector('.logout-btn');
    if (logoutBtn) {
        logoutBtn.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            logoutUser();
        });
    }
});
    </script>
</body>
</html>

        // Set current date
        document.querySelector('.current-date').textContent = new Date().toLocaleDateString('id-ID', {
            weekday: 'long',
            year: 'numeric',
            month: 'long',
            day: 'numeric'
        });
        
        // Initialize current month in filter
        const currentDate = new Date();
        const currentMonth = currentDate.getFullYear() + '-' + String(currentDate.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0');
        document.getElementById('periodeFilter').value = currentMonth;
        
        // Filter button event
        document.getElementById('filterBtn').addEventListener('click', function() {
            const status = document.getElementById('statusFilter').value;
            const ukm = document.getElementById('ukmFilter').value;
            const periode = document.getElementById('periodeFilter').value;
            
            // Show loading indicator
            const originalText = this.innerHTML;
            this.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-spinner fa-spin"></i> Memproses...';
            this.disabled = true;
            
            // Simulate API call
            setTimeout(() => {
                alert(`Filter diterapkan:\nStatus: ${status}\nUKM: ${ukm}\nPeriode: ${periode}`);
                
                // Reset button
                this.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-filter"></i> Terapkan Filter';
                this.disabled = false;
            }, 500);
        });
        
        // Tab functionality
        function showProposalTab(tabName) {
            // Hide all tabs
            document.querySelectorAll('.proposal-content').forEach(tab => {
                tab.style.display = 'none';
            });
            
            // Remove active class from all buttons
            document.querySelectorAll('.proposal-tab').forEach(btn => {
                btn.classList.remove('active');
            });
            
            // Show selected tab
            document.getElementById(`${tabName}-proposals`).style.display = 'block';
            
            // Add active class to clicked button
            event.target.classList.add('active');
            
            // Show message for other tabs
            if (tabName !== 'pending') {
                document.getElementById(`${tabName}-proposals`).innerHTML = `
                    <div style="text-align: center; padding: 60px 20px;">
                        <i class="fas fa-clipboard-list" style="font-size: 48px; color: #ddd; margin-bottom: 20px;"></i>
                        <h3 style="color: #666; margin-bottom: 10px;">Proposal ${tabName === 'approved' ? 'Disetujui' : tabName === 'rejected' ? 'Ditolak' : 'Revisi'}</h3>
                        <p style="color: #999;">Daftar proposal ${tabName === 'approved' ? 'yang telah disetujui' : tabName === 'rejected' ? 'yang ditolak' : 'yang membutuhkan revisi'}</p>
                        <p style="color: #999; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 20px;">Gunakan tabel di bawah untuk melihat detail proposal</p>
                    </div>
                `;
            }
        }
        
        // Proposal actions
        function approveProposal(proposalId) {
            if (confirm(`Setujui proposal ${proposalId}? Dana akan dialokasikan.`)) {
                // Show loading
                const approveBtn = event.target;
                const originalText = approveBtn.innerHTML;
                approveBtn.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-spinner fa-spin"></i> Memproses...';
                approveBtn.disabled = true;
                
                // Simulate API call
                setTimeout(() => {
                    alert(`Proposal ${proposalId} berhasil disetujui`);
                    approveBtn.innerHTML = originalText;
                    approveBtn.disabled = false;
                    
                    // Update UI
                    document.querySelector('.proposal-status').innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-check-circle"></i> Disetujui';
                    document.querySelector('.proposal-status').className = 'proposal-status status-approved';
                    
                    // Disable action buttons
                    document.querySelectorAll('.action-buttons .btn').forEach(btn => {
                        btn.disabled = true;
                    });
                }, 1000);
            }
        }
        
        function rejectProposal(proposalId) {
            const reason = prompt('Masukkan alasan penolakan:');
            if (reason) {
                // Show loading
                const rejectBtn = event.target;
                const originalText = rejectBtn.innerHTML;
                rejectBtn.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-spinner fa-spin"></i> Memproses...';
                rejectBtn.disabled = true;
                
                // Simulate API call
                setTimeout(() => {
                    alert(`Proposal ${proposalId} ditolak: ${reason}`);
                    rejectBtn.innerHTML = originalText;
                    rejectBtn.disabled = false;
                    
                    // Update UI
                    document.querySelector('.proposal-status').innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-times-circle"></i> Ditolak';
                    document.querySelector('.proposal-status').className = 'proposal-status status-rejected';
                    
                    // Disable action buttons
                    document.querySelectorAll('.action-buttons .btn').forEach(btn => {
                        btn.disabled = true;
                    });
                }, 1000);
            }
        }
        
        function requestRevision(proposalId) {
            const note = prompt('Masukkan catatan revisi:');
            if (note) {
                // Show loading
                const revisionBtn = event.target;
                const originalText = revisionBtn.innerHTML;
                revisionBtn.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-spinner fa-spin"></i> Memproses...';
                revisionBtn.disabled = true;
                
                // Simulate API call
                setTimeout(() => {
                    alert(`Revisi diminta untuk proposal ${proposalId}: ${note}`);
                    revisionBtn.innerHTML = originalText;
                    revisionBtn.disabled = false;
                    
                    // Update UI
                    document.querySelector('.proposal-status').innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-edit"></i> Perlu Revisi';
                    document.querySelector('.proposal-status').className = 'proposal-status status-revised';
                }, 1000);
            }
        }
        
        function deferReview(proposalId) {
            const date = prompt('Tunda hingga tanggal (DD/MM/YYYY):');
            if (date) {
                alert(`Review proposal ${proposalId} ditunda hingga: ${date}`);
                // In real app, you would make an API call here
            }
        }
        
        function viewProposal(proposalId) {
            alert(`Melihat detail proposal: ${proposalId}`);
            // In real app, you would load the proposal details
        }
        
        function viewDocument(docName) {
            alert(`Membuka dokumen: ${docName}`);
            // In real app, you would open the document in a modal or new tab
        }
        
        function submitComment() {
            const commentInput = document.getElementById('commentInput');
            const comment = commentInput.value.trim();
            
            if (!comment) {
                alert('Silakan masukkan komentar terlebih dahulu');
                return;
            }
            
            // Show loading
            const submitBtn = event.target;
            const originalText = submitBtn.innerHTML;
            submitBtn.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-spinner fa-spin"></i> Mengirim...';
            submitBtn.disabled = true;
            
            // Simulate API call
            setTimeout(() => {
                // Add new comment to the list
                const commentsContainer = document.querySelector('.review-comments');
                const newComment = document.createElement('div');
                newComment.className = 'comment-item';
                newComment.innerHTML = `
                    <div class="comment-header">
                        <strong>Admin Keuangan</strong>
                        <small>${new Date().toLocaleDateString('id-ID', { day: '2-digit', month: 'short', year: 'numeric' })} ${new Date().toLocaleTimeString('id-ID', { hour: '2-digit', minute: '2-digit' })}</small>
                    </div>
                    <p>${comment}</p>
                `;
                
                // Insert before the comment input section
                commentsContainer.insertBefore(newComment, commentsContainer.children[commentsContainer.children.length - 1]);
                
                // Clear input
                commentInput.value = '';
                
                // Reset button
                submitBtn.innerHTML = originalText;
                submitBtn.disabled = false;
                
                alert('Komentar berhasil dikirim');
            }, 500);
        }
        
        function exportProposals() {
            alert('Data proposal akan diexport ke Excel');
            // In real app, you would trigger file download
        }
        
        // Initialize tab visibility
        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
            // Show pending tab by default, hide others
            document.getElementById('pending-proposals').style.display = 'block';
            
            // Hide other tabs initially
            const tabs = ['approved', 'rejected', 'revised'];
            tabs.forEach(tab => {
                const tabElement = document.getElementById(`${tab}-proposals`);
                if (tabElement) {
                    tabElement.style.display = 'none';
                }
            });
        });
        // Fungsi logout sederhana
function logoutUser() {
    if (confirm('Apakah Anda yakin ingin logout?')) {
        // Hapus data sesi
        localStorage.removeItem('user');
        localStorage.removeItem('loginTime');
        
        // Redirect ke halaman login
        window.location.href = 'index.html';
    }
}

// Atur event listener untuk tombol logout
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
    const logoutBtn = document.querySelector('.logout-btn');
    if (logoutBtn) {
        logoutBtn.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            logoutUser();
        });
    }
});
    </script>
</body>
</html>
```

                                        <button class="btn btn-sm btn-info" onclick="viewTransaction('TRX-2024-0009')">
                                            <i class="fas fa-eye"></i>
                                        </button>
                                    </td>
                                </tr>
                                <tr>
                                    <td>TRX-2024-0008</td>
                                    <td>UKM Fotografi</td>
                                    <td>Rp 1.500.000</td>
                                    <td>Perlengkapan</td>
                                    <td>24 Jan 2024</td>
                                    <td><span class="status status-rejected">Ditolak</span></td>
                                    <td>
                                        <button class="btn btn-sm btn-info" onclick="viewTransaction('TRX-2024-0008')">
                                            <i class="fas fa-eye"></i>
                                        </button>
                                    </td>
                                </tr>
                            </tbody>
                        </table>
                    </div>
                    
                    <div style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between; align-items: center; margin-top: 20px;">
                        <div style="font-size: 14px; color: #666;">
                            Menampilkan 1-5 dari 188 transaksi
                        </div>
                        <div class="pagination">
                            <button class="btn btn-secondary btn-sm" disabled>
                                <i class="fas fa-chevron-left"></i>
                            </button>
                            <span style="margin: 0 10px;">Halaman 1 dari 38</span>
                            <button class="btn btn-secondary btn-sm">
                                <i class="fas fa-chevron-right"></i>
                            </button>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                </div>
            </div>
        </main>
    </div>
    
    <script>
        // Set current date
        document.querySelector('.current-date').textContent = new Date().toLocaleDateString('id-ID', {
            weekday: 'long',
            year: 'numeric',
            month: 'long',
            day: 'numeric'
        });
        
        // Set today's date as default filter
        document.getElementById('filterDate').valueAsDate = new Date();
        
        // Tab functionality
        function showTab(tabName) {
            // Hide all tabs
            document.querySelectorAll('.tab-content').forEach(tab => {
                tab.classList.remove('active');
            });
            
            // Remove active class from all buttons
            document.querySelectorAll('.tab-btn').forEach(btn => {
                btn.classList.remove('active');
            });
            
            // Show selected tab
            document.getElementById(`${tabName}-tab`).classList.add('active');
            
            // Add active class to clicked button
            event.target.classList.add('active');
        }
        
        // Filter transactions
        document.getElementById('applyFilterBtn').addEventListener('click', function() {
            const status = document.getElementById('filterStatus').value;
            const ukm = document.getElementById('filterUKM').value;
            const date = document.getElementById('filterDate').value;
            const amount = document.getElementById('filterAmount').value;
            
            // Show loading indicator
            const originalText = this.innerHTML;
            this.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-spinner fa-spin"></i> Memproses...';
            this.disabled = true;
            
            // Simulate API call
            setTimeout(() => {
                alert(`Filter diterapkan:\nStatus: ${status}\nUKM: ${ukm}\nTanggal: ${date}\nJumlah: ${amount}`);
                
                // Reset button
                this.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-filter"></i> Terapkan';
                this.disabled = false;
            }, 500);
        });
        
        // Transaction actions
        function verifyTransaction(trxId) {
            if (confirm(`Verifikasi transaksi ${trxId}?`)) {
                // Show loading
                alert(`Transaksi ${trxId} berhasil diverifikasi`);
                // In real app, you would make an API call here
            }
        }
        
        function rejectTransaction(trxId) {
            const reason = prompt('Masukkan alasan penolakan:');
            if (reason) {
                alert(`Transaksi ${trxId} ditolak: ${reason}`);
                // In real app, you would make an API call here
            }
        }
        
        function requestRevision(trxId) {
            const note = prompt('Masukkan catatan revisi:');
            if (note) {
                alert(`Revisi diminta untuk transaksi ${trxId}: ${note}`);
                // In real app, you would make an API call here
            }
        }
        
        function viewDocument(docName) {
            alert(`Membuka dokumen: ${docName}`);
            // In real app, you would open the document in a modal or new tab
        }
        
        function viewTransaction(trxId) {
            alert(`Melihat detail transaksi ${trxId}`);
            // In real app, you would show detailed view in a modal
        }
        
        // Bulk actions
        function bulkVerify() {
            const selected = document.querySelectorAll('.transaction-check:checked');
            if (selected.length === 0) {
                alert('Pilih minimal satu transaksi');
                return;
            }
            
            if (confirm(`Verifikasi ${selected.length} transaksi terpilih?`)) {
                alert(`${selected.length} transaksi berhasil diverifikasi`);
                // In real app, you would make an API call here
            }
        }
        
        function bulkReject() {
            const selected = document.querySelectorAll('.transaction-check:checked');
            if (selected.length === 0) {
                alert('Pilih minimal satu transaksi');
                return;
            }
            
            const reason = prompt('Masukkan alasan penolakan untuk semua transaksi:');
            if (reason) {
                alert(`${selected.length} transaksi ditolak: ${reason}`);
                // In real app, you would make an API call here
            }
        }
        
        function clearSelection() {
            document.querySelectorAll('.transaction-check').forEach(checkbox => {
                checkbox.checked = false;
            });
            alert('Semua pilihan dibatalkan');
        }
        
        // Export transactions
        function exportTransactions(type) {
            const typeName = type === 'verified' ? 'terverifikasi' : 
                           type === 'rejected' ? 'ditolak' : 'semua';
            alert(`Data transaksi ${typeName} akan diexport ke Excel`);
            // In real app, you would trigger file download
        }
        
        // Initialize tab content visibility
        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
            // Show pending tab by default
            showTab('pending');
        });
        // Fungsi logout sederhana
function logoutUser() {
    if (confirm('Apakah Anda yakin ingin logout?')) {
        // Hapus data sesi
        localStorage.removeItem('user');
        localStorage.removeItem('loginTime');
        
        // Redirect ke halaman login
        window.location.href = 'index.html';
    }
}

// Atur event listener untuk tombol logout
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
    const logoutBtn = document.querySelector('.logout-btn');
    if (logoutBtn) {
        logoutBtn.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            logoutUser();
        });
    }
});
    </script>
</body>
</html>
```

        // Set current date

            weekday: 'long',
            year: 'numeric',
            month: 'long',
            day: 'numeric'
        });
        
        // Filter button event
        document.getElementById('filterBtn').addEventListener('click', function() {
            const periode = document.getElementById('periode').value;
            const ukm = document.getElementById('ukm').value;
            const kategori = document.getElementById('kategori').value;
            
            alert(`Filter diterapkan:\nPeriode: ${periode}\nUKM: ${ukm}\nKategori: ${kategori}`);
        });
        
        // Export button event
        document.getElementById('exportBtn').addEventListener('click', function() {
            alert('Laporan keuangan berhasil diexport ke format Excel!');
        });
        
        // Initialize select values
        document.getElementById('periode').value = 'year';
        // Fungsi logout sederhana
function logoutUser() {
    if (confirm('Apakah Anda yakin ingin logout?')) {
        // Hapus data sesi
        localStorage.removeItem('user');
        localStorage.removeItem('loginTime');
        
        // Redirect ke halaman login
        window.location.href = 'index.html';
    }
}

// Atur event listener untuk tombol logout
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
    const logoutBtn = document.querySelector('.logout-btn');
    if (logoutBtn) {
        logoutBtn.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            logoutUser();
        });
    }
});
    </script>
</body>
</html>
```

    <div id="uploadModal" class="modal-overlay" style="display: none;">
        <div class="modal-content">
            <div class="modal-header">

                    <!-- File list akan muncul di sini -->
                </div>

                <button class="btn btn-primary" onclick="processUpload()">Unggah</button>

    </div>
    
    <script>
        // Set current date
        document.querySelector('.current-date').textContent = new Date().toLocaleDateString('id-ID', {
            weekday: 'long',
            year: 'numeric',
            month: 'long',
            day: 'numeric'
        });
        
        // Filter documents
        function filterDocuments(category) {
            // Update active filter tag
            document.querySelectorAll('.filter-tag').forEach(tag => {
                tag.classList.remove('active');
            });
            event.target.classList.add('active');
            
            // Filter documents
            const cards = document.querySelectorAll('.document-card');
            cards.forEach(card => {
                if (category === 'all' || card.dataset.category === category) {
                    card.style.display = 'block';
                } else {
                    card.style.display = 'none';
                }
            });
            
            alert(`Menampilkan dokumen kategori: ${category}`);
        }
        
        // Search documents
        function searchDocuments() {
            const query = document.querySelector('.search-input').value;
            if (query.trim()) {
                alert(`Mencari dokumen: ${query}`);
                // Implement search logic
            }
        }
        
        // Document actions
        function viewDocument(docName) {
            alert(`Membuka dokumen: ${docName}`);
            // Implement document viewer
        }
        
        function downloadDocument(docName) {
            alert(`Mengunduh dokumen: ${docName}`);
            // Implement download logic
        }
        
        function shareDocument(docName) {
            alert(`Berbagi dokumen: ${docName}`);
            // Implement share logic
        }
        
        function editDocument(docName) {
            alert(`Mengedit dokumen: ${docName}`);
            // Implement edit logic
        }
        
        function validateDocument(docName) {
            if (confirm(`Validasi dokumen ${docName}?`)) {
                alert(`Dokumen ${docName} telah divalidasi`);
                // Implement validation logic
            }
        }
        
        function archiveDocument(docName) {
            if (confirm(`Arsipkan dokumen ${docName}?`)) {
                alert(`Dokumen ${docName} telah diarsipkan`);
                // Implement archive logic
            }
        }
        
        function requestAccess(docName) {
            alert(`Meminta akses untuk dokumen: ${docName}`);
            // Implement access request logic
        }
        
        // Upload modal functions
        function showUploadModal() {
            document.getElementById('uploadModal').style.display = 'flex';
        }
        
        function closeUploadModal() {
            document.getElementById('uploadModal').style.display = 'none';
            document.getElementById('uploadFileList').innerHTML = '';
        }
        
        function triggerFileUpload() {
            document.getElementById('fileUpload').click();
        }
        
        function handleFileUpload() {
            const files = document.getElementById('fileUpload').files;
            const fileList = document.getElementById('uploadFileList');
            fileList.innerHTML = '';
            
            for (let i = 0; i < files.length; i++) {
                const fileItem = document.createElement('div');
                fileItem.className = 'file-item';
                fileItem.innerHTML = `
                    <div>
                        <strong>${files[i].name}</strong>
                        <small>${formatFileSize(files[i].size)}</small>
                    </div>
                    <button class="btn btn-sm btn-danger" onclick="removeFile(${i})">
                        <i class="fas fa-times"></i>
                    </button>
                `;
                fileList.appendChild(fileItem);
            }
        }
        
        function removeFile(index) {
            // Implement file removal logic
            alert(`Menghapus file index: ${index}`);
        }
        
        function processUpload() {
            alert('Memproses upload file...');
            closeUploadModal();
        }
        
        // Toggle view
        function toggleView() {
            const button = event.target.closest('button');
            const cards = document.querySelector('.document-cards');
            const table = document.querySelector('.table-container');
            
            if (cards.style.display !== 'none') {
                cards.style.display = 'none';
                table.style.display = 'block';
                button.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-th-large"></i> Tampilan Kartu';
            } else {
                cards.style.display = 'grid';
                table.style.display = 'block';
                button.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-th"></i> Tampilan Grid';
            }
        }
        
        // Utility functions
        function formatFileSize(bytes) {
            if (bytes === 0) return '0 Bytes';
            const k = 1024;
            const sizes = ['Bytes', 'KB', 'MB', 'GB'];
            const i = Math.floor(Math.log(bytes) / Math.log(k));
            return parseFloat((bytes / Math.pow(k, i)).toFixed(2)) + ' ' + sizes[i];
        }
        // Fungsi logout sederhana
function logoutUser() {
    if (confirm('Apakah Anda yakin ingin logout?')) {
        // Hapus data sesi
        localStorage.removeItem('user');
        localStorage.removeItem('loginTime');
        
        // Redirect ke halaman login
        window.location.href = 'index.html';
    }
}

// Atur event listener untuk tombol logout
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
    const logoutBtn = document.querySelector('.logout-btn');
    if (logoutBtn) {
        logoutBtn.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            logoutUser();
        });
    }
});
    </script>
</body>
</html>
```

---

### 6.8. audit-admin.html
```html
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="id">

        }

        }
        
        .logout-btn i {
            margin-right: 8px;
        }
        
        /* Main Content Styles */
        .main-content {
            flex: 1;
            margin-left: 260px;
            padding: 20px;
            width: calc(100% - 260px);
            min-height: 100vh;
            background: #f5f7fa;
        }

                            <i class="fas fa-eye"></i> Lihat
                        </button>
                        <button class="btn btn-secondary btn-sm" onclick="downloadReport('multimedia-2023')">
                            <i class="fas fa-download"></i> Unduh
                        </button>
                    </div>
                </div>
            </div>
            
            <!-- Audit Checklist -->
            <div class="audit-checklist">
                <h3>Checklist Audit Keuangan</h3>
                <div class="checklist-list">
                    <div class="checklist-item">
                        <input type="checkbox" class="checklist-checkbox" id="check1" checked>
                        <div class="checklist-content">
                            <div style="font-weight: 500;">Validasi dokumen pendukung transaksi</div>
                            <small>Memastikan semua transaksi memiliki bukti dokumen yang valid</small>
                        </div>
                        <span class="checklist-status status-approved">Selesai</span>
                    </div>
                    
                    <div class="checklist-item">
                        <input type="checkbox" class="checklist-checkbox" id="check2" checked>
                        <div class="checklist-content">
                            <div style="font-weight: 500;">Verifikasi kesesuaian dengan anggaran</div>
                            <small>Memeriksa apakah pengeluaran sesuai dengan anggaran yang disetujui</small>
                        </div>
                        <span class="checklist-status status-approved">Selesai</span>
                    </div>
                    
                    <div class="checklist-item">
                        <input type="checkbox" class="checklist-checkbox" id="check3">
                        <div class="checklist-content">
                            <div style="font-weight: 500;">Review laporan keuangan bulanan</div>
                            <small>Memeriksa kelengkapan dan akurasi laporan keuangan</small>
                        </div>
                        <span class="checklist-status status-pending">Dalam Proses</span>
                    </div>
                    
                    <div class="checklist-item">
                        <input type="checkbox" class="checklist-checkbox" id="check4">
                        <div class="checklist-content">
                            <div style="font-weight: 500;">Evaluasi sistem pengendalian internal</div>
                            <small>Menilai efektivitas sistem pengendalian keuangan UKM</small>
                        </div>
                        <span class="checklist-status status-pending">Belum Dimulai</span>
                    </div>
                </div>
            </div>
        </main>
    </div>
    
    <script>
        // Set current date
        document.querySelector('.current-date').textContent = new Date().toLocaleDateString('id-ID', {
            weekday: 'long',
            year: 'numeric',
            month: 'long',
            day: 'numeric'
        });
        
        // Audit functions
        function startNewAudit() {
            alert('Memulai audit baru...');
            // Implement new audit logic
        }
        
        function generateAuditReport() {
            alert('Membuat laporan audit...');
            // Implement report generation
        }
        
        function scheduleAudit() {
            alert('Menjadwalkan audit...');
            // Implement schedule logic
        }
        
        function viewCriticalFindings() {
            alert('Menampilkan temuan kritis...');
            // Implement critical findings view
        }
        
        function auditSettings() {
            alert('Membuka pengaturan audit...');
            // Implement settings logic
        }
        
        function viewAudit(auditId) {
            alert(`Melihat audit: ${auditId}`);
            // Implement audit view
        }
        
        function viewReport(reportId) {
            alert(`Melihat laporan: ${reportId}`);
            // Implement report view
        }
        
        function downloadReport(reportId) {
            alert(`Mengunduh laporan: ${reportId}`);
            // Implement download logic
        }
        
        // Findings functions
        function assignInvestigation(findingId) {
            const investigator = prompt('Tugaskan investigasi kepada:');
            if (investigator) {
                alert(`Investigasi untuk temuan ${findingId} ditugaskan kepada: ${investigator}`);
                // Implement assignment logic
            }
        }
        
        function requestAction(findingId) {
            const action = prompt('Minta tindakan untuk:');
            if (action) {
                alert(`Tindakan diminta untuk temuan ${findingId}: ${action}`);
                // Implement action request
            }
        }
        
        function viewDetails(findingId) {
            alert(`Menampilkan detail temuan: ${findingId}`);
            // Implement detail view
        }
        
        function sendReminder(findingId) {
            alert(`Mengirim pengingat untuk temuan: ${findingId}`);
            // Implement reminder logic
        }
        
        function provideTemplate(findingId) {
            alert(`Menyediakan template untuk temuan: ${findingId}`);
            // Implement template provision
        }
        
        function exportFindings() {
            alert('Mengekspor temuan audit...');
            // Implement export logic
        }
        
        // Checklist functionality
        document.querySelectorAll('.checklist-checkbox').forEach(checkbox => {
            checkbox.addEventListener('change', function() {
                const checklistItem = this.closest('.checklist-item');
                const statusSpan = checklistItem.querySelector('.checklist-status');
                
                if (this.checked) {
                    statusSpan.textContent = 'Selesai';
                    statusSpan.className = 'checklist-status status-approved';
                } else {
                    statusSpan.textContent = 'Belum Dimulai';
                    statusSpan.className = 'checklist-status status-pending';
                }
            });
        });
        // Fungsi logout sederhana
function logoutUser() {
    if (confirm('Apakah Anda yakin ingin logout?')) {
        // Hapus data sesi
        localStorage.removeItem('user');
        localStorage.removeItem('loginTime');
        
        // Redirect ke halaman login
        window.location.href = 'index.html';
    }
}

// Atur event listener untuk tombol logout
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
    const logoutBtn = document.querySelector('.logout-btn');
    if (logoutBtn) {
        logoutBtn.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            logoutUser();
        });
    }
});
    </script>
</body>
</html>
```
